			add_province_modifier = {
				static_modifiers = { animate_forest }
				province = { id = 5978 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = { 
			ROOT = { controls_province = 6347 }
		}
		998 = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				static_modifiers = { animate_forest }
				province = { id = 6347 }
			}
		}
	}
	
}
